/****** Object:  UserDefinedFunction [dbo].[GetIndianDate]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
Create Function [dbo].[GetIndianDate]()
RETURNS DateTime
As
BEGIN
              return(Cast(SWITCHOFFSET(SYSDATETIMEOFFSET(), '+05:30') as datetime))
End
GO

 CONSTRAINT [PK__SMmp_Use__0A618CBC893BC26F] PRIMARY KEY CLUSTERED 
(
	[UserMenuMappingID] ASC
)WITH (PAD_INDEX = OFF, STATISTICS_NORECOMPUTE = OFF, IGNORE_DUP_KEY = OFF, ALLOW_ROW_LOCKS = ON, ALLOW_PAGE_LOCKS = ON, OPTIMIZE_FOR_SEQUENTIAL_KEY = OFF) ON [PRIMARY]

/****** Object:  View [Tyache].[VMmp_UserMenuMapping]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE View [Tyache].[VMmp_UserMenuMapping]
as
	Select  UMM.UserID,
			UMM.MenuID, 
			LoginID, 
			DisplayName, 
			Ltrim(rtrim(MenuName)) as MenuName,
			ShortFormName,
			FilterOption1,
			FilterOption2,
			FilterOption4,
			FilterOption3,
			LoadingDevice
	From SMmp_UserMenuMapping UMM 
	Join SMst_User UM on UM.UserID = UMM.UserID
	Join SMst_Menu MM on MM.MenuID = UMM.MenuID 
	where UMM.IsValid = 1
GO

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[Report_RePrintingLog]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

create Procedure [SLR].[Report_RePrintingLog]
@FromDate	date ,
@ToDate		date

As
Begin
	Select 
		   ProductCode
		  ,ProductName
		  ,BatchNumber
		  ,DLNumber
		  ,GrossWeight
		  ,TareWeight
		  ,NetWeight
		  ,MfgDate
		  ,ExpDate
		  ,UPCNo
		  ,Storage
		  ,DrumNumber
		  ,LabelCode
		  ,RP.LabelName
		  ,PrinterName
		  ,RP.SerialNumber
		  ,Rp.Username
		  ,RP.ComputerName
		  ,RP.TransTime as PrintedOn

		  --- Select columns for CSV Data

	  FROM LOU_Datatech.SLR.STra_Reprint RP
	  join SLR.STra_PrintPlan PP on PP.PlanID = RP.PlanID
	  where CONVERT(date,RP.TransTime) between CONVERT(date,@FromDate) and CONVERT(date,@ToDate)
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_Get_AssignedMenuList]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [SLR].[SP_Get_AssignedMenuList]
@UserID		bigint

As
Begin	
	Begin
		Select  UMM.MenuID,
				MenuName 
		From [SLR].SMmp_UserMenuMapping UMM 
		join [SLR].SMst_User UM on UM.UserID = UMM.UserID
		Join [SLR].SMst_Menu MM on MM.MenuID = UMM.MenuID 
		where UMM.IsValid = 1 and UM.UserID = @UserID and LoadingDevice='D'
	End
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_Get_MenuList]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [SLR].[SP_Get_MenuList]

@UserID		int

As
Begin 

		SELECT M.[MenuID],
				[MenuName]
		FROM [SLR].[SMst_Menu] M
		left join [SLR].SMmp_UserMenuMapping UM on M.MenuID = UM.MenuID and UM.UserID = @UserID and UM.IsValid = 1
		where  UM.MenuID is  null
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_Get_UserList]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [SLR].[SP_Get_UserList]
@IsActive	varchar(30)

As
Begin
	SELECT
		[LoginID],
		[UserID] ,
		DisplayName
	FROM [SLR].[SMst_User] 
	Where IsActive = @IsActive 
			--and LoginID like '%' + @LoginID + '%'
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_InsertPrinterAssignment]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

create Procedure [SLR].[SP_InsertPrinterAssignment]
@Workstation		varchar(100),
@Process			varchar(50),
@PrinterName		varchar(100),
@MessBox			varchar(100) Out 

AS


Begin
	If @Workstation <> '' and @Process <> '' and @PrinterName <> ''
	Begin
		If (Select count(PrinterID) from SLR.SMst_PrinterManagement where ComputerName = @Workstation and Process = @Process) = 0
		Begin
			Insert into SLR.SMst_PrinterManagement (ComputerName ,Process , PrinterName, TransTime)
			Values (@Workstation ,@Process , @PrinterName , dbo.GetIndianDate() )
		
			Set @MessBox = 'Success : Workstation - printer assignment configured : work station - ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '# printer name - ' + isnull(@Process , '') 

		End
		Else
		Begin

			Update SLR.SMst_PrinterManagement 
				set PrinterName = @PrinterName 
			where ComputerName = @Workstation 
				and Process = @Process

			Set @MessBox = 'Sucess  : Workstation - printer name updated : work station - ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '# printer name - ' + isnull(@Process , '') 

		End
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Set @MessBox = 'Warning : Invalid data  ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '#' + isnull(@Process,'')
	End
End
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [SLR].[SP_InsertUpdateUser]
@LoginID		Varchar(100),
@DisplayName	Varchar(100),
@IsActive		bit,
@TransUserID	Bigint,
@TransSessionID	Bigint,
@MessBox		Varchar(2000) OUT

As
SET NOCOUNT ON
Declare @UserID	int


SET @MessBox	= 'Warning : Not a Valid Input'

--Select @PlantID = PlantID FRom SMst_Plant where PlantCode = @PlantCode

Begin Tran	
	If @LoginID <> ''
	Begin
		IF (Select count(*) from [SLR].SMst_User where LoginID = @LoginID and isactive = 1  ) = 0
		BEGIN
			Insert into [SLR].SMst_User 
					(LoginID,DisplayName ,TransUserID,TranssessionID,TransTime,IsActive,Isvalid)
			Values
					(@LoginID,@DisplayName ,@TransUserID,@TransSessionID,dbo.GetIndianDate(), 1,@IsActive)

			Select @UserID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()
			
			

			SET @MessBox='Success : New User Sucessfully Added : ' + CONVERT(varchar(30),@UserID)

		Commit Tran
		END
		ELSE
		BEGIN			
				Update [SLR].SMst_User set 
				DisplayName		= @DisplayName,
				IsValid			=	@IsActive,
				TransSessionID	=	@TransSessionID,
				TransUserID		=	@TransUserID
				where LoginID	= @LoginID

				SET @MessBox='Success : User details updated for LoginID : ' + @LoginID
			Commit Tran
		END
	End
	Else
	Begin
		
		SET @MessBox='Warning : Invalid LoginID  ' + @LoginID
	End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_InsertUpdateUserMenuMapping]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE procedure [SLR].[SP_InsertUpdateUserMenuMapping]
@UserID			bigint,
@MenuID			bigint,
@TransUserID	bigint,
@TransSessionID bigint,
@MessBox		varchar(2000)OUT

AS 
SET NOCOUNT ON;
Declare @UserRights as bigint

BEGIN
	
	If (Select count(UserID) from [SLR].SMst_User where UserID = @UserID and IsActive = 1) = 1
	Begin
		If (Select count(UserMenuMappingID) from [SLR].SMmp_UserMenuMapping where UserID= @UserID and MenuID=@MenuID and IsValid=1) = 0
		Begin
		
			Insert into [SLR].SMmp_UserMenuMapping 
					(UserID,MenuID,TransUserID,TransSessionID,TransTime,IsValid) 
			Values
					(@UserID,@MenuID,@TransUserID,@TransSessionID,dbo.GetIndianDate(),1)

			Set	@MessBox ='User Rights Provided Successfully !! '+ convert(varchar(50),@MenuID)
		End
		Else
		Begin
		
			Set	@MessBox ='Warning : User Rights Already Exist !! ' + convert(varchar(50),@MenuID)

		End                    
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Set	@MessBox ='Warning : User status is InActive to assign authorities  : ' + convert(varchar(50),@MenuID)
	End
END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_Login]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE PROCEDURE [SLR].[SP_Login]
@ComputerName		Varchar(50),
@SystemUserName		Varchar(50),
@LoginID			Varchar(100),
@OutStatus			Varchar(100) Out,
@MessBox			Varchar(500) Out,
@TransSessionID		bigint out,
@TransUserID		bigint out

As
SET NOCOUNT ON
Set		@OutStatus = '100'

Begin Tran

	Select  @TransUserID = UserID From [SLR].SMst_User Where LoginID = @LoginID and IsActive = 1

	IF @TransUserID is null
	BEGIN
		Set @OutStatus= 'InValid'
		Set @MessBox  ='Warning : ' + @LoginID + ' Authorized User Login'
	commit tran
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Insert into [SLR].STra_SessionLog 
				(SystemUserName,ComputerName,LoginName,LoginUserID,LoginTime) 
		Values 
				(@SystemUserName,@ComputerName,@LoginID,@TransUserID,dbo.GetIndianDate())

		Select @TransSessionID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

		Set @OutStatus= 'Success'
		SET @MessBox='Authorized User : ' + @LoginID + ' SessionID : ' + CONVERT(varchar(30),@TransSessionID)
		
		Commit Tran
	END
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [SLR].[SP_Print]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [SLR].[SP_Print]
@PlanID			bigint ,
@LabelName		varchar(100) ,
@PrinterName	varchar(100) ,
@TransUserID	bigint ,
@TransSessionID	bigint ,
@UserName		varchar(100)  ,
@ComputerName	varchar(100)  ,
@MessBox		varchar(200) out ,
@ValidPrint		varchar(10) out ,
@SerialNumber	bigint Out

As
Begin
Declare @PrintAutoID	bigint 

	If (Select COUNT(PlanID) from SLR.STra_PrintPlan where PlanID = @PlanID and IsValid = 1) > 0
	Begin
			Select @SerialNumber = isnull(SerialNumber , 0) + 1 from SLR.STra_LastSerialNumber 

			Insert into SLR.STra_PrintingLog (PlanID , LabelName , PrinterName , SerialNumber , Username , ComputerName , TransUserID , TransSessionID , TransTime)
			Values (@PlanID , @LabelName , @PrinterName , @SerialNumber , @UserName , @ComputerName , @TransUserID , @TransSessionID  , dbo.GetIndianDate())

			Select @PrintAutoID = SCOPE_IDENTITY ()

			Update SLR.STra_PrintPlan set isValid = 0 where PlanID = @PlanID 

			Update SLR.STra_LastSerialNumber set SerialNumber = @SerialNumber 

			Insert into SLR.SLog_Print ( PrintAutoID , EventType , EventDescription , UserName , ComputerName , TransUserID , TransSessionID , TransTime  )
			Values (@PrintAutoID , 'Start Print' , 'Start Label Printing' , @UserName , @ComputerName , @TransUserID , @TransSessionID , dbo.GetIndianDate() )

			Set @ValidPrint = 'True'
			Set @MessBox	= 'Success : Label Print'
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Set @ValidPrint = 'True'
		Set @MessBox	= 'Warning  : Invalid plan to print label ' + ISNULL(CONVERT(Varchar(10) , @PlanID),'')
	End

End


GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[Report_PrintingLog]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[Report_PrintingLog]
@FromDate	date ,
@ToDate		date

As
Begin
	Select 
		   ProductCode
		  ,ProductName
		  ,BatchNumber
		  ,DLNumber
		  ,GrossWeight
		  ,TareWeight
		  ,NetWeight
		  ,MfgDate
		  ,ExpDate
		  ,UPCNo
		  ,Storage
		  ,ContainerNumber
		  ,CaseNo
		  ,LabelCode
		  ,LabelName
		  ,PrinterName
		  ,SerialNumber
		  ,Username
		  ,ComputerName
		  ,PL.TransTime as PrintedOn
		,Convert(Varchar(300),ProductCode)	+ ',' + 
       Convert(Varchar(300),ProductName)	+ ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(300),BatchNumber)	+ ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(300),DLNumber)	+ ',' +
       CAST(GrossWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CAST(TareWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CAST(NetWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), MfgDate, 120) + ',' + -- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD format
       CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), ExpDate, 120) + ',' + -- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD format
       --Convert(Varchar(50),  UPCNo) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(500),  Storage) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  ContainerNumber) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  CaseNo) + ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(50),  LabelCode) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  LabelName) + ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  PrinterName) + ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(50),  SerialNumber)  --+ ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  Username) + ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  ComputerName) + ',' +
       -- CONVERT(VARCHAR(19), PL.TransTime, 120) 
	   AS CSVData

		  --- Select columns for CSV Data

	  FROM LOU_Datatech.Tyache.STra_PrintingLog PL
	  join Tyache.STra_PrintPlan PP on PP.PlanID = PL.PlanID
	  where CONVERT(date,PL.TransTime) between CONVERT(date,@FromDate) and CONVERT(date,@ToDate)
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[Report_RePrintingLog]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[Report_RePrintingLog]
@FromDate	date ,
@ToDate		date

As
Begin
	Select 
		   ProductCode
		  ,ProductName
		  ,BatchNumber
		  ,DLNumber
		  ,GrossWeight
		  ,TareWeight
		  ,NetWeight
		  ,MfgDate
		  ,ExpDate
		  ,UPCNo
		  ,Storage
		  ,ContainerNumber
		  ,CaseNo
		  ,LabelCode
		  ,RP.LabelName
		  ,PrinterName
		  ,RP.SerialNumber
		  ,Rp.Username
		  ,RP.ComputerName
		  ,RP.TransTime as PrintedOn
		  ,Convert(Varchar(300),ProductCode)	+ ',' + 
       Convert(Varchar(300),ProductName)	+ ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(300),BatchNumber)	+ ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(300),DLNumber)	+ ',' +
       CAST(GrossWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CAST(TareWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CAST(NetWeight AS VARCHAR(50)) + ',' +
       CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), MfgDate, 120) + ',' + -- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD format
       CONVERT(VARCHAR(100), ExpDate, 120) + ',' + -- Convert to YYYY-MM-DD format
       --Convert(Varchar(50),  UPCNo) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(500),  Storage) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  ContainerNumber) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  CaseNo) + ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(50),  LabelCode) + ',' +
        Convert(Varchar(50),  RP.LabelName) + ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  PrinterName) + ',' +
       Convert(Varchar(50),  SerialNumber)  --+ ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  Username) + ',' +
       -- Convert(Varchar(50),  ComputerName) + ',' +
       -- CONVERT(VARCHAR(19), PL.TransTime, 120) 
	   AS CSVData
		  --- Select columns for CSV Data

	  FROM LOU_Datatech.Tyache.STra_Reprint RP
	  join Tyache.STra_PrintPlan PP on PP.PlanID = RP.PlanID
	  where CONVERT(date,RP.TransTime) between CONVERT(date,@FromDate) and CONVERT(date,@ToDate)
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[SP_Get_AssignedMenuList]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[SP_Get_AssignedMenuList]
@UserID		bigint

As
Begin	
	Begin
		Select  UMM.MenuID,
				MenuName 
		From [Tyache].SMmp_UserMenuMapping UMM 
		join [Tyache].SMst_User UM on UM.UserID = UMM.UserID
		Join [Tyache].SMst_Menu MM on MM.MenuID = UMM.MenuID 
		where UMM.IsValid = 1 and UM.UserID = @UserID and LoadingDevice='D'
	End
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[SP_Get_MenuList]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO
CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[SP_Get_MenuList]

@UserID		int

As
Begin 

		SELECT M.[MenuID],
				[MenuName]
		FROM [Tyache].[SMst_Menu] M
		left join [Tyache].SMmp_UserMenuMapping UM on M.MenuID = UM.MenuID and UM.UserID = @UserID and UM.IsValid = 1
		where  UM.MenuID is  null
End
GO

CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[SP_Get_UserList]
@IsActive	bit

As
Begin
	SELECT
		[LoginID],
		[UserID] ,
		DisplayName
	FROM [Tyache].[SMst_User] 
	Where IsActive = @IsActive 
			--and LoginID like '%' + @LoginID + '%'
End

/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[SP_InsertPrinterAssignment]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/

GO

Create Procedure [Tyache].[SP_InsertPrinterAssignment]
@Workstation		varchar(100),
@Process			varchar(50),
@PrinterName		varchar(100),
@MessBox			varchar(100) Out 

AS


Begin
	If @Workstation <> '' and @Process <> '' and @PrinterName <> ''
	Begin
		If (Select count(PrinterID) from Tyache.SMst_PrinterManagement where ComputerName = @Workstation and Process = @Process) = 0
		Begin
			Insert into Tyache.SMst_PrinterManagement (ComputerName ,Process , PrinterName, TransTime)
			Values (@Workstation ,@Process , @PrinterName , dbo.GetIndianDate() )
		
			Set @MessBox = 'Success : Workstation - printer assignment configured : work station - ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '# printer name - ' + isnull(@Process , '') 

		End
		Else
		Begin

			Update Tyache.SMst_PrinterManagement 
				set PrinterName = @PrinterName 
			where ComputerName = @Workstation 
				and Process = @Process

			Set @MessBox = 'Sucess  : Workstation - printer name updated : work station - ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '# printer name - ' + isnull(@Process , '') 

		End
	End
	Else
	Begin
		Set @MessBox = 'Warning : Invalid data  ' + isnull(@Workstation,'') + '#' + isnull(@Process,'')
	End
End
GO
/****** Object:  StoredProcedure [Tyache].[SP_InsertRePrint]    Script Date: 6/27/2024 9:54:32 PM ******/
SET ANSI_NULLS ON
GO
SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON
GO

CREATE Procedure [Tyache].[SP_InsertRePrint]
@PlanID					bigint ,
@PrintAutoID			bigint ,
@SerialNumber			bigint ,
@LabelName				varchar(50) ,
@Remark					varchar(100) ,
@PrinterName			varchar(100) ,
@UserName				varchar(100) ,
@ComputerName			varchar(100) ,
@TransUserID			bigint ,
@TransSessionID			bigint,
@MessBox				varchar(200) out ,
@ValidPrint				varchar(10) out 

As
Begin
Set noCount On;
Declare @RePrintID		bigint 

		If (Select COUNT(PlanID) from Tyache.STra_PrintPlan where PlanID = @PlanID and IsValid = 0) > 0
		Begin
			If (Select COUNT(PrintAutoID) from Tyache.STra_PrintingLog where PrintAutoID = @PrintAutoID ) > 0
			Begin
				Insert into Tyache.STra_Reprint(PlanID , PrintAutoID , LabelName , SerialNumber ,Remark , PrinterName , Username , ComputerName , TransUserID , TransSessionID , TransTime)
				Values (@PlanID , @PrintAutoID , @LabelName ,@SerialNumber, @Remark , @PrinterName ,@UserName , @ComputerName , @TransUserID , @TransSessionID  , dbo.GetIndianDate())

				Select @RePrintID = SCOPE_IDENTITY ()

				Update Tyache.STra_PrintPlan set isValid = 0 where PlanID = @PlanID 

				Insert into Tyache.SLog_RePrint ( RePrintID , PlanID , PrintAutoID , EventType , EventDescription ,LabelName , Remark , PrinterName , Username , ComputerName , TransUserID , TransSessionID , TransTime  )
				Values (@RePrintID , @PlanID ,@PrintAutoID ,'Start Print' , 'Start Label Printing' ,@LabelName ,  @Remark , @PrinterName , @UserName , @ComputerName , @TransUserID , @TransSessionID , dbo.GetIndianDate() )

				
				Set @MessBox	= 'Success : Label RePrint'
				Set @ValidPrint = 'True'
			End
			Else
			Begin
				Set @MessBox	= 'Warning : Invalid Printing Information To RePrint ;  ' + ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar(10), @PrintAutoID),'')
				Set @ValidPrint = 'False'
			End
		End
		Else
		Begin
			Set @MessBox	= 'Warning : Invalid Printing Plan To RePrint ;  ' + ISNULL(CONVERT(varchar(10), @PlanID),'')
			Set @ValidPrint = 'False'
		End
End
GO
